      924 followers
    </span>

<div class="pv-recent-activity-section-v2__summary t-14 t-black--light t-normal">
  <div class="pv-recent-activity-section-v2__columns">

            <li id="ember143" class="pv-recent-activity-item-v2 pv-recent-activity-item-v2--expanded ember-view">  <a class="app-aware-link pv-recent-activity-item-v2__detail" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/update/urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6798010413482090496">
    <div class="pv-recent-activity-item-v2__entity-logo
        ">
      <div class="ivm-image-view-model   ">
    <div class="ivm-view-attr__img-wrapper ivm-view-attr__img-wrapper--use-img-tag display-flex

<!---->      <img width="56" src="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE6RxxTIEz4PQ/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1611612883191?e=1632960000&amp;v=beta&amp;t=4-KEszH7VkfaUj3MMTmXttScRYbvUSEcNcWpNw03usQ" loading="lazy" height="56" alt="View Jithin Pradeeps profile" id="ember144" class="ivm-view-attr__img--centered EntityPhoto-circle-4 pv-recent-activity-item-v2__image lazy-image ember-view">
</div>
  </div>
<!---->    </div>
    <div class="pv-recent-activity-item-v2__summary-info">
        <h3 class="pv-recent-activity-item-v2__title t-16 t-black t-bold break-words">
          <div class="inline-show-more-text
    inline-show-more-text--is-collapsed
    inline-show-more-text--is-collapsed-with-line-clamp
    
    
    " style="line-height:2.4rem;max-height:4.8rem;-webkit-line-clamp:2;">

    Happy to share that our #acl2021 findings paper 'Learning Robust Latent Representations for Controllable Speech Synthesis' is now available at https://lnkd.in/efUhZC5 (draft). Here we show that small changes in Transformers like layer reordering and new mutual info terms can lead to accelerated convergence and stability in style control. 

I'd like to congratulate the co-authors Hussain Zaidi, Jithin Pradeep and thank my supervisor Gerald Penn, Annie Lee for their helpful comments and reviews. This paper forms part of our 8 month applied research in the Master of Science in Applied Computing program. Shout out to Claire Mosses for making sure our masters was always on track : )
  
<!---->
<!----></div>
        </h3>
        <div class="pv-recent-activity-item-v2__message t-14 t-black t-normal">
          <div class="inline-show-more-text
    inline-show-more-text--is-collapsed
